             </div>
             <div class="sbSocialShare sbEmail sbShow">
              <i class="fa fa-envelope-o" onclick="window.location.href = 'mailto:dan@neweurope.eu';return false;">
              </i>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="sbR">
            <div class="sbGraph">
             <canvas class="sbGraphCanvas" data-sbdata="26,26,51,51,26,26,26,26,51,51,26,51,51,51,51,26,55,30,26,51,51,26,51,26,51,51,51,26,26,26,51,51,26,51,26,26,51,51,51,51,51,51,51,51,51,51,30,51,51,51" height="50" id="sbGraphCanvas2" width="150">
             </canvas>

            <div class="sbGraphInfo sbTip" data-tip="The New Europe social meter measures how quickly our readers share this article on social media.">
             What's this?
            </div>

           <div class="sbClr">
           </div>
          </div>
          <script type="text/javascript">
           var sbFBAPPID = '1621095111443198';
          </script>
          <p>
           The Russia-EU summits used to be splendid opportunities for pictures and grandiose declarations, always spreading over two days, and comprising a dinnerincluding Russian president Vladimir Putin, the president of the Commission Jose Manuel Barroso, the presidentof the Council Herman Van Rompuy, and manyother EU high officials. More often than not, they would be called historic by the president of the Commission Barroso, who makes an immoderate use of theword.
          </p>
          <p>
           But Tuesdays 32nd EU-Russia summit will now consist of a meeting of only a couple of hours. On 28 January, Putin is supposed to arrive by 13.30, and a pressconference is already announced for 16.00 h.
          </p>
          <p>
           EU officials wouldnt comment on this, but the drastic downgrading of the summit reflects Putins displeasure with the EUs position on Ukraine and on manyother issues, including Syria.
          </p>
          <p>
           The displeasure is so high, that, as demonstrative gesture, no concrete topic will be discussed during the meeting, leaving the Europeans wondering how to draftthe final communique. One formula already circulating is that theparticipants will proceed to an in-depthreflection about the EU-Russia relationship.
          </p>
          <div id="fb_voice_src" style=" text-align: center;  margin-left: -150px;  float: left;  margin-bottom: 10px;">
           <a href="#socialbuzz-bottom-infinite-view-232156">
            <img src="http://www.neurope.eu/wp-content/themes/exquisite-wp-child/img/voice.png"/>
           </a>
          </div>
          <style>
           .fcbk_share{float: left;  width: 170px;}
          </style>
          <div class="fcbk_share">
           <div class="fcbk_like">
            <div id="fb-root">
            </div>
            <script>
             (function(d, s, id) {
								var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
								if (d.getElementById(id)) return;
								js = d.createElement(s); js.id = id;
								js.src = "//connect.facebook.net/en_US/sdk.js#xfbml=1&amp;appId=1443946719181573&amp;version=v2.0";

							}(document, "script", "facebook-jssdk"));
            </script>
            <fb:like href="http://www.neurope.eu/article/eu-and-russia-tense-summit/" layout="button_count" share="false" show_faces="false" width="450">
            </fb:like>
           </div>
          </div>
          <script>
           jQuery(document).ready(function() {jQuery("#fb_voice_src a").smoothScroll({offset: -100});});
          </script>
          <p>
           The year 2013 saw a strengthening of Putins attitude vis-a-vis the EU and the West in general. The tone of Russias diplomacy becamemore nationalistic andaggressive, and on key international issues, such as the war in Syria, or the Iranian nuclear dossier, Russia systematically blockedimportant Western decisions.
          </p>
          <p>
           In the case of Syria, where it holds its only military naval point in the Mediterranean, Moscow established itself openly as the protector of the Assad dynasticregime, who managed to cling to power until now mostly thanks to Russian (and Iranian) backing.
          </p>
          <p>
           By providing temporary political asylum to the former CIA agent Edward Snowden Putin showed that his decisions cannot be influenced by US pressure.In hisrelations with Europe, Putin scored by torpedoing the EUs Nabucco gas pipeline project, and by emptying of substance the EUs EasternPartnership, destinedto six former Soviet republics. From these six, only Moldova did notyetfall back into Russias sphere of influence. Belorussia andArmenia joined a CustomsUnion with Russia and Kazakhstan, Georgia and Ukraine announced that they might do the same, while Azerbaijan remains anauthoritarian regime havingclose ties with Moscow. That is the reason why Moldova has been promised the quick lifting of the visa obligation for itscitizens, something that Russia is farfrom being able to obtain.
          </p>
          <p>
           Putin could also touch the subject of the EU enquiry into the commercial practices of Gazprom, the Russian energy trust, while the visa regimecould alsoimposeitself on Tuesdays summits agenda. EU officials could hardly make any promise of a liberalisation of the visa regime, given the recent changes inRussianlegislation leading to a de-factostigmatisation of the LGBT community.
          </p>
          <p>
           Putin did not improve the atmosphere last week by assuring that he does not have any problems with homosexuals: They can come to the Sochi Olympics nextmonth  so long as they stay away from children.
          </p>
          <p>
           Also last week, preceding Putins visit, Russian Commissioner for Human Rights Konstantin Dolgov presented in Brussels the Russian Ministry of ForeignAffairs Report on the Human Rights Situation in the EU. The report tried to paint a less than rosy picture ofthe state of basic human rights in most EUcountries, as if to prevent major Western criticism against Russia itself on the eve of the Sochi Olympic games. Asked about the report, EU officials wouldntcomment on it, saying that Putin is free to use it in hisdiscussions with the Barroso-Van Rompuy duo.
          </p>
          <p>
           It was already announced that no important EU Commissioner will attend the opening of the Sochi games, in spite of the invitations having been sent a long timein advance, officially because of the overcharged agendas.
          </p>
          <p>
           And, finally, Ukraine will be a major topic of the talks. Last November, Russian pressure forced Ukraine to suspend the signing of an Association agreement withthe EU. Since then, the standoff between the government and protesters has been permanent, with at least threedead and hundreds of wounded recorded untilnow. Still, with the exception of Lithuania, the only EU country proposing that a list of sanctions be drafted, practically all the other member states remain for thetime being opposed to imposing sanctions to Ukraine.
          </p>
          <p>
           Last week,Ukrainian Prime Minister Mykola Azarov, who had travelled to the World Economic Forum in Davos, Switzerland, to defend the regimes actions wasprevented by the Davos organisers to enter the congress hall. It is the only such instance in thehistory of the Davos World Economic Forum.
          </p>
          <p>
           
          </p>
          <p>
          </p>

  function fa_mail_reply_click(){
	 jQuery(".fa-google-plus").hide();
	 jQuery(".fa-linkedin").hide();
	 jQuery(".fa-reddit").hide();
	 jQuery(".fa-mail-forward").show();
	 jQuery(".fa-mail-reply").hide();	 
  }

  function fa_search_click(){
	 jQuery(".fa-close").show();
	 jQuery(".fa-search").hide();	 
	 jQuery(".persistent-header-reading-now").hide();	
	 jQuery(".persistent-header__social.showable.show").hide();
	 jQuery(".persistent-header__content-container .searchform").show();
  }

  function fa_close_click(){
	 jQuery(".fa-close").hide();
	 jQuery(".persistent-header__content-container .searchform").hide();
	 jQuery(".persistent-header-reading-now").show();	
	 jQuery(".persistent-header__social.showable.show").show();
	 jQuery(".fa-search").show();	 
  }
  
  

var cureent_slide ;
var cureent_slide_homeSlide; 
function adjustWindow_next(){
	 
	 // Init Skrollr
	 var s = skrollr.init();
	 
	 // Get window size
	  winH = $window.height();
	  
	  // Keep minimum height 550
	  if(winH &lt;= 680) {
		 winH = 680;
	 } 
	  
	  // Resize our slides
	  cureent_slide.height(winH);
	  
	  // Refresh Skrollr after resizing our sections
	  s.refresh(jQuery('.'+cureent_slide_homeSlide));
	  
}


jQuery(document).ready(function() {
	jQuery(".fancybox").fancybox();
	// Setup variables
	$window = jQuery(window);
	$slide = jQuery('.homeSlide_232156');
	$body = jQuery('#main_parallax_enabled');
	//FadeIn all sections   
	$body.imagesLoaded( function() {
		setTimeout(function() {
		      
		      // Resize sections
		      adjustWindow();
		      
		      // Fade in sections
			  $body.removeClass('loading').addClass('loaded');
			  jQuery('.image-caption').css('visibility','visible');
			  if(jQuery('#main_parallax_enabled').hasClass("loaded") &amp;&amp; jQuery('#lede_image').length &gt; 0 ){
				  var lede_image_distance = jQuery('#lede_image').height()+jQuery('#lede_image').offset().top;
				  var doc_distance = jQuery(document).scrollTop();
				  if (doc_distance &lt;= lede_image_distance) {
					  jQuery(".pushdowns-not-visible .leftRailWrapper").css("top",(lede_image_distance-doc_distance-57)+"px");
				  }
				  else{
					 jQuery(".pushdowns-not-visible .leftRailWrapper").css("top","0px");
				  }
				}
		}, 800);
	});
	var waypoint_ini = new Waypoint({
	 element: document.getElementById('socialbuzz-top-'+infiniteScroll_real_current_post_id),
	 handler: function(direction) {
		 
		 var $elem = jQuery('#socialbuzz-top-'+infiniteScroll_real_current_post_id);
		 var $window = jQuery(window);
	
		 var docViewTop = $window.scrollTop();
		 var docViewBottom = docViewTop + $window.height();
	
		 var elemTop = $elem.offset().top;
		 var elemBottom = elemTop + $elem.height()-100;
		 
		 var $elem1 = jQuery('#socialbuzz-bottom-'+infiniteScroll_real_current_post_id);
	
		 var elemTop1 = $elem1.offset().top;
		 var elemBottom1 = elemTop1 + $elem1.height();				
	
		 var judge_val = ((elemBottom &lt;= docViewTop) &amp;&amp; (elemTop1 &gt;= docViewBottom));
		 
		 if (direction == 'down') {
			 if (judge_val) {
				 jQuery("#vertical-social-"+infiniteScroll_real_current_post_id).fadeIn( 300);
			 }
			 
		 }
		 else if (direction == 'up') {
			 elemBottom = elemBottom + 50;
			 judge_val = ((elemBottom &lt;= docViewTop) &amp;&amp; (elemTop1 &gt;= docViewBottom));
			 if (!judge_val) {
				 jQuery("#vertical-social-"+infiniteScroll_real_current_post_id).fadeOut( 300);
			 }
		 }
	 },
	 offset: 0
  });
 
  var waypoint_ini_2 = new Waypoint({
	 element: document.getElementById('socialbuzz-bottom-'+infiniteScroll_real_current_post_id),
	 handler: function(direction) {
		 
		 var $elem = jQuery('#socialbuzz-top-'+infiniteScroll_real_current_post_id);
		 var $window = jQuery(window);
	
		 var docViewTop = $window.scrollTop();
		 var docViewBottom = docViewTop + $window.height();
	
		 var elemTop = $elem.offset().top;
		 var elemBottom = elemTop + $elem.height();
		 
		 var $elem1 = jQuery('#socialbuzz-bottom-'+infiniteScroll_real_current_post_id);
	
		 var elemTop1 = $elem1.offset().top;
		 var elemBottom1 = elemTop1 + $elem1.height();				
	
		 var judge_val = ((elemBottom &lt;= docViewTop) &amp;&amp; (elemTop1 &gt;= docViewBottom));
		 
		 if (direction == 'up') {
			 if (judge_val) {
				 jQuery("#vertical-social-"+infiniteScroll_real_current_post_id).fadeIn( 300);
			 }
		 }
		 else if (direction == 'down') {
			 if (!judge_val) {
				 jQuery("#vertical-social-"+infiniteScroll_real_current_post_id).fadeOut( 300);
			 }
		 }
	 },
	 offset: 'bottom-in-view'
  });
  
	function adjustWindow(){
		
		// Init Skrollr
		var s = skrollr.init();
		
		// Get window size
	    winH = $window.height();
	    
	    // Keep minimum height 550
	    if(winH &lt;= 550) {
			winH = 550;
		} 
	    
	    // Resize our slides
	    $slide.height(winH);
	    
	    // Refresh Skrollr after resizing our sections
	    s.refresh(jQuery('.homeSlide'));
	    
	}
  
});
